## 💡 Tips for Accelerated Learning
1. **Thematic Association (Clustering)**: Learning words grouped by subject improves memory retention by linking new terms to familiar mental models.
2. **Focus on Collocations & Sentences**: Read the example sentence provided for each word to understand real-world context and preposition usage.
3. **Spaced Repetition (SRS)**: Pick 1 or 2 categories per day, test active recall on definitions, and review them 1 day, 3 days, and 7 days later.

| 344 | **witch** | `/wɪtʃ/` | *Noun* | A woman thought to have magical powers, typically evil ones. | The folklore tells of a powerful witch who could control the weather. |

## ⏰ Time, Dates, Seasons & Frequency (252 Words)

| # | Word | Pronunciation (IPA) | Part of Speech | Primary Meaning | Example Sentence |
| :---: | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 1 | **abrupt** | `/əˈbrʌpt/` | *Adjective* | Sudden and unexpected. | The train's abrupt stop threw passengers forward. |
